proclam


wherea act congress th june enact
indian titl land lie state
missouri missouri river extinguish jurisdict
said land cede said act state missouri
western boundari said state extend
missouri river reserv unit state origin right
soil said land dispos

wherea said act provid
take effect presid proclam declar
indian titl said land extinguish state
missouri assent provis said act

wherea act pass gener assembl state
missouri th decemb express assent
said state provis said act congress copi
act gener assembl duli authent
offici commun govern file
depart state

now therefor martin van buren presid unit state
america proclam declar make known
indian titl said land lie state missouri
missouri river extinguish said act
congress th june take effect date hereof

given hand citi washington th day march
ad independ unit state america
sixtyfirst

martin van buren
